</th>

</td></tr>

<h5> <span class="mw-headline" id="For_2_Trumpets_and_2_Trombones_.28Bach-Rondeau.29_2">For 2 Trumpets and 2 Trombones (Bach-Rondeau)</span></h5>
<div class="we"><div id="IMSLP247290" class="we_file_first we_fileblock_14">
